if (!is_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle') != '3fca23e0ccc7b21a123b47a968c81703a930b0aa') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_example_data_oracle', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle') !== '3fca23e0ccc7b21a123b47a968c81703a930b0aa') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle') !== '54abdd16cc0b68de0b354d898e6434b1ee038bd1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_example_data_oracle')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_example_data_oracle', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_oracle') !== '3fca23e0ccc7b21a123b47a968c81703a930b0aa') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_example_data_oracle');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') != 'ea32aed0d4e95ba395af3b030439f13e2aa1063e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== 'ea32aed0d4e95ba395af3b030439f13e2aa1063e') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== '9d95b0bd525f46e167c15d614686a20246855554') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== 'ea32aed0d4e95ba395af3b030439f13e2aa1063e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
		}
	}
}
